***отражать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отражать.html>отража́ть</a> (5069)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отразить.html>отрази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otrazítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отражать.html>отража́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otražátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отразить.html>отрази́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to repel, to ward off, to refute, to parry</li>
<li>to reflect, to mirror</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разить.html>рази́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отражение.html>отраже́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otražénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отражать.html>отража́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otražátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отражаться.html>отража́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otražátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отразиться.html>отрази́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be reflected, to reverberate</li>
<li>to affect, to have an impact <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> on</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отражать.html>отража́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otražátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отразить.html>отрази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otrazítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отражение.html>отраже́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otražénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отражение.html>отраже́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отражение.html>отраже́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отражение.html>отраже́ний</a></b>)

***отразить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отразить.html>отрази́ть</a> (11628)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разить.html>рази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отразить.html>отрази́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otrazítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отражать.html>отража́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to repel, to ward off, to refute, to parry</li>
<li>to reflect, to mirror</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отразить.html>отрази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otrazítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отразиться.html>отрази́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otrazítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отражаться.html>отража́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be reflected, to reverberate</li>
<li>to affect, to have an impact <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> on</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отразить.html>отрази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otrazítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***отрегулировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отрегулировать.html>отрегули́ровать</a> (27748)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:регулировать.html>регули́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">regulírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрегулировать.html>отрегули́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otregulírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:регулировать.html>регули́ровать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to adjust, to regulate, to tune up</li></ol>

<p>Deverbal noun from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрезать.html>отре́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otrézatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрез.html>отре́з</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otréz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрез.html>отре́за</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрез.html>отре́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрез.html>отре́зов</a></b>)

***отрезать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отрезать.html>отреза́ть</a> (2727)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резать.html>ре́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rézatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрезать.html>отре́зать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otrézatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрезать.html>отреза́ть</a></strong></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the impf./pf. forms differ in the word stress in the infinitive and the conjugation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to cut off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:семь.html>семь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отмерить.html>отме́рь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отрезать.html>отре́жь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">semʹ raz otmérʹ, odín otréžʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">look before you leap</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрезать.html>отреза́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>пути́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otrezatʹ putí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">close the door, <a href = vnd.unilang:бар.html>bar</a> the way</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to snip off</li>
<li>to divide, to apportion</li>
<li><i>(speech)</i> to cut short, to snap out</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрезать.html>отре́зать</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otrézatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-atʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрезать.html>отреза́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otrezátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрезать.html>отре́зать</a></strong></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the impf./pf. forms differ in the word stress in the infinitive and the conjugation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to cut off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:семь.html>семь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отмерить.html>отме́рь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:отрезать.html>отре́жь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">semʹ raz otmérʹ, odín — otréžʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">look before you leap</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрезать.html>отреза́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>пути́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otrezatʹ putí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">close the door, <a href = vnd.unilang:бар.html>bar</a> the way</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to snip off</li>
<li>to divide, to apportion</li>
<li><i>(speech)</i> to cut short, to snap out</li></ol>

***отрекаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отрекаться.html>отрека́ться</a> (19217)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">отрек-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otrek-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-atʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрекаться.html>отрека́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otrekátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отречься.html>отре́чься</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to disown, to disavow, to renounce, to give up, to repudiate</li>
<li>to abdicate</li></ol>

***отречение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отречение.html>отрече́ние</a> (24286)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отречение.html>отрече́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otrečénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отречение.html>отрече́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отречение.html>отрече́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отречение.html>отрече́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>renunciation</li>
<li>abdication</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***отречься.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отречься.html>отре́чься</a> (12372)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>речь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rečʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отречься.html>отре́чься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otréčʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрекаться.html>отрека́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to disown, to disavow, to renounce, to give up, to repudiate</li>
<li>to abdicate</li></ol>
